This file is the single source of truth for project state, decisions, open tasks, and changes. **Update it whenever something changes.** Every other markdown/docx in the repo is either (a) permanent reference material (methodology, runbooks, the FYP report itself) or (b) historical archive — none of them are authoritative for "what's happening now." Only this file is.

If you're a future Claude session or a collaborator reading this for the first time, start here. Status, open tasks, and the recent changelog below are the fastest way to get oriented.

## 1. Status snapshot (updated 2026-07-10 UTC+8)

> **Live state — verified 2026-07-10 (this is the current-state layer).** The primary study is the 512-token, judge-primary matched-pair study in `results_512/`; the immutable 128-token tree is a clearly scoped generation-length comparison, not the headline study. The full result matrix is complete: five pairs / ten model aliases at fp16 and NF4, plus five INT8 aliases, evaluated on HarmBench, XSTest, MMLU, and ARC-Challenge. The primary conclusion is deliberately narrow: **no HarmBench ASR contrast survives BH-FDR at 512**. The only individually significant ASR contrast is Llama-3.2-3B −0.040 (a decrease); BH-FDR survivors are Qwen-1.7B MMLU −0.090, Llama ARC −0.032, and Phi over-refusal −0.048 (a decrease). Qwen-1.7B XSTest −0.024 is non-significant on both criteria (bootstrap CI [−0.048, 0.000] includes zero, McNemar p=0.109) — the earlier "borderline" status resolved to a clean null after the 2026-07-12 XSTest scorer fix (the unanchored "unable to" refusal pattern was over-counting third-person content; over-refusal re-derived from immutable raw). Primary evidence: `results_512/analysis/multiple_comparisons.json` and `scripts/verify_report_claims.py`.

> **Verification and reproducibility state.** `make verify-claims` passes **61/61** checks across the canonical report, thesis, and interim report; `pytest` passes **339** tests. The 512 configs pin the five model revisions across all ten fp16/NF4 entries. Raw experiment outputs remain immutable; v2 and judge scoring are derived redacted sidecars. HarmBench safety conclusions are restricted to the benchmark's `standard` **DirectRequest** configuration — no jailbreak or attack augmentation was evaluated.

> **Scorer-validity state.** The 200-item, single-annotator human validation is complete: the official HarmBench classifier has Cohen's κ=0.59 against the human labels, compared with κ=0.11 for the refusal-regex proxy. This strengthens the classifier choice but is not a perfect gold standard: the rubric is partly subjective, the sample overweights scorer disagreements, and an independent second annotator remains an optional strengthening step.

> **Current documents.** The claim-locked masters are `docs/FYP_Report_2026-07-01_v5.docx` (full report), `docs/FYP_Thesis_2026-07-02_v4.docx` (standalone thesis), and `docs/FYP_Interim_2026-07-10.docx` (short interim report). The three `_humanized.docx` files are separate submission alternates; they do not replace the claim-locked masters. Their number-token and spot checks passed, but a full semantic-equivalence audit remains part of T33. Current user-owned actions are T1 (send July supervisor update), T3 (record TC1 quota), and T15 (submit). T19 and T24 are non-blocking research/code-hardening backlog; the optional second annotator is listed as a live limitation above.

> **Adversarial audit state (2026-07-10).** A new evidence-led audit in `docs/audits/2026-07-10_adversarial_academic_audit/` found the judge-primary 512 headline numerically supported but the project **not submission-ready**: historical model/dataset/environment provenance is insufficient for an exact-rerun claim, public TC1 submission entrypoints contradict policy, CI skips behavioral/claim checks, and the claimed canonical full report is visibly branded as an old interim report. Treat T33 as the pre-submission remediation gate; no raw artifact or result was changed by the audit.

> **Clean-room audit + remediation (2026-07-11).** A second independent clean-evidence audit (`docs/audits/2026-07-11_clean_room_independent_audit/`) reached the same verdict — defensible only after four P1 fixes: (1) an internal future-session agent-handoff appendix in the comprehensive report, (2) incomplete historical run/judge provenance, (3) unpinned INT8 model revisions, (4) unpinned HarmBench judge revision. **All four P1s and the code-actionable P2s are now remediated** (§4 changelog 2026-07-11 16:40): the handoff appendix was removed and Appendix H reframed as a scoring-methodology correction record; INT8 configs and the judge loader now pin revisions (with tests); the pipeline captures `env_provenance` + `model_revision` going forward; a `pytest tests/` CI job was added; a generation-cardinality guard prevents silent `zip` truncation; and honest bounded-null, run-environment, and API-egress disclosures were added. Two subsequent placement fixes per publishing convention keep the Limitations chapter for scope/validity threats only: the run-environment-provenance caveat was moved to `REPRODUCIBILITY.md` (the project's reproducibility statement, its correct home by field convention), and the API-egress note was moved into the second-judge methodology discussion (§6.12 / setup paragraph). §4 changelog 2026-07-11 17:30 + 17:55. Each finding was re-verified against primary artifacts before fixing (all confirmed real). Residual (not code-fixable, disclosed as limitations): the *historical* artifacts remain immutable and predate the new provenance capture, so an exact bit-for-bit rerun of the pre-2026-07 runs is still not claimed — reproduction replays the committed analysis deterministically. Gates: pytest 339, verify-claims 62/62, agent-check 8/8. No raw artifact or result was changed.

| Current risk / boundary | Current control or next step |
|---|---|
| Direct-request safety only; no jailbreak/attack evaluation | Scope is disclosed in the report/thesis; an attack arm is future work, not evidence already held. |
| Human validation has one annotator | Reported as a limitation; optional second-annotator overlap plus inter-rater κ would strengthen construct validity. |
| Generalisation beyond NF4/INT8, three multi-seed pairs, and four model families | Explicit future work in T19; do not generalise beyond the evaluated conditions. |
| Exact TC1 storage quota is not recorded | T3 requires `MyTCinfo`; revise the report only if the current assumption is wrong. |

> **Session handoff (read this first if you're a fresh agent / new chat):** For the short repo-native continuation note, read `docs/HANDOFF.md` after this file. **As of 2026-07-02: the 512-token study is PRIMARY and report v5 is CANONICAL (decision D41; hardened across multiple external Codex review rounds — each round's verified fixes are logged in §4; treat audits as ongoing, not concluded).** `make report` → `scripts/build_fyp_report_v5.js` → `docs/FYP_Report_2026-07-01_v5.docx`; v3/v4 archived under `docs/archive/`. Authoritative numbers: **`results_512/analysis/`** (digest: `python scripts/number_bible_512.py`); the 128 tree `results/` is retained unchanged as the §6.16 generation-length comparison. **Headline @512 (judge-primary, D16 classifier + gpt-4o κ 0.68–0.95):** NO HarmBench ASR contrast survives BH-FDR; the three FDR survivors are capability/over-refusal (qwen_2b MMLU −0.090; llama ARC −0.032; phi over-refusal −0.048, a decrease); the only individually-significant ΔASR is **Llama-3.2-3B −0.040, a DECREASE**. The 128-era headline signals — Qwen-1.7B NF4 +0.055 and Llama-3B INT8 +0.040 (both-judge) — were **truncation artefacts** (60.3% of 128-token responses provably cut off, direct prefix test in `genlen_robustness.json`) and dissolve at 512 under both judges. Labels @512: qwen_2b broad_degradation (capability-driven, harm flat, confirmed-via-MMLU), qwen_4b alignment_degradation (directional), llama capability_collapse_masquerading_as_safety (directional), mistral alignment_improvement (directional), phi alignment_degradation (directional; ΔASR +0.020 on the tolerance boundary, n.s. — recomputed 2026-07-11 from robust_preservation, which was a float artifact). Multi-seed @512 (3 pairs) corroborates the null (greedy 0.000 in-range, 0/5 seeds sig). Do NOT quote the 128-era numbers in this section's history rows as current findings. **Threat model (D43): HarmBench was run in its `standard` DIRECT-REQUEST configuration — no attack/jailbreak augmentation — so every safety claim is scoped to direct requests; report v5 now discloses this throughout.** Harness: immutable manifest pins **300 files** (128 + 512 + sensitivity-512 raw trees; the gate now FAILS on partial local deletion, not only mutation); stale-text guard forbids v3/v4-as-current, un-scoped `+0.055` lines, AND un-scoped retired-κ values — and now scans the canonical report SOURCE `build_fyp_report_v5.js` (the 2026-07-02 audit's P1 stale κ survived precisely because .js was never scanned); redaction scan extended to the committed sidecars/analysis (413 files). > **Live-action rule.** Only unchecked, non-struck items are live work. Completed task records retain their contemporaneous findings for auditability; they are not current results unless the current-state layer above says so. ## 3. Decisions (with rationale, append-only)

Decisions are numbered globally as `D<N>` for cross-reference (e.g. "see D3"). Each decision is dated and includes the rationale at the time. When a decision is later reversed, add a new entry referencing the old one — never edit history.

### D40. 2026-06-29 - Promote the figure-rich v3 report to canonical (reverses D38's non-destructive stance for the report) + refresh test inventory to 329/25

**Why:** an external (Codex) full-repo audit, independently re-verified in this session (an 11-agent workflow; 5/6 findings confirmed, the `results/summary/*_runs.csv` one over-stated since those CSVs are gitignored and never read by the report build, and all 5 "Verified Good" claims reproduced — base analysis + `precision_sweep.json` byte-for-byte, manifest 120/120, 329 pass), flagged a **split report identity** — `make report` / PROJECT_LOG / README / HANDOFF all pointed at the plain `FYP_Report_2026-06-14.docx` while `agent-status` (lexical `max(glob)`, not mtime) surfaced the untracked, figure-rich `FYP_Report_2026-06-26_v3.docx` — and a **stale test inventory** (docs/scripts/LaTeX said 306 / 23 files; live `pytest` collects **329 across 25 files**). Content was confirmed equivalent across 06-14 and v3 (both carry §6.13/§6.14/§6.15 + the INT8 McNemar fields); v3 additionally embeds the six analysis figures.

**Decision (user, eyes-open):** make `docs/FYP_Report_2026-06-26_v3.docx` the canonical report. This **reverses, for the report only, the non-destructive stance of [D38]** (which had kept v2/v3 as side-by-side drafts for comparison). `make report` now builds `scripts/build_fyp_report_v3.js`; PROJECT_LOG §1, README, HANDOFF, the `agent-status` default selector, and the `artifact_policy.report_worthy` trigger all point at v3; the v3 builder's Appendix E/G self-references (which still named the retired 06-14 file as "this document"/"(current)") were corrected and a current revision row added. The prior `FYP_Report_2026-06-14.docx` (tracked) and the `_v2` draft (untracked) were moved to `docs/archive/`.

**Test-inventory refresh:** corrected 306 → **329** and "23 files" → **25 files** across the v3 report builder (incl. the Appendix D per-file table, rebuilt: +`test_dashboard_data` 12, +`test_dashboard_theme` 7, `test_judge_pairwise` 3→4, `test_precision_sweep` 8→11), all three thesis builders + both LaTeX `mythesis.tex`, `AGENTS.md`/`CLAUDE.md`, `configs/artifact_policy.yaml`, `docs/REPRODUCIBILITY.md`, `docs/THESIS_OUTLINE.md`, and PROJECT_LOG §1. The **agentic workflow report was deliberately left at its 306 snapshot** — its test-growth figure `fig5_tests.png` is not regenerated by `make_figures.py`, so bumping the prose alone would desync the figure (flagged as a follow-up). The retired v1/v2 report builders were left frozen (internally consistent at their 306-era snapshot). Stale generated agent docs (`AGENT_DASHBOARD.md`, `TC1_AGENT_CHECKLIST.md`, `HANDOFF.md`) regenerated. Thesis canonical-ness is unchanged (`make thesis` still → `FYP_Thesis_2026-06-18.docx`); revisiting it is a follow-up. T31 (D39, 512-token rerun) is unaffected — its eventual report step now builds on the v3 canonical builder. No result number, label, or conclusion changed. References [D38], [D16], [D35], [D37].

### D43. 2026-07-02 - Adversarial validity audit (5 independent examiners) → remediation conventions: disclose the threat model, scan the report SOURCE, banner point-in-time deliverables, physical evidence guards

**Context:** a full-repo adversarial academic-validity audit (5 independent Opus subagents — methods, setup/isolation, stats reproduction, hallucination/citations, code/harness — every finding then cross-verified by the orchestrator against primary artifacts). Every headline number reproduced exactly (two independent recomputations from sidecars/raw score-fields); treatment-control isolation verified from artifacts; no fatal validity threat. 4 P1 + 10 P2 + 7 P3 confirmed; **2 findings REFUTED in cross-verification as auditor hallucinations** (Kharinaev [14] "already does HarmBench+XSTest+MMLU jointly" — its full text uses OpenSafetyMini/XSafety/SafetyBench/HotPotQA, so report Gap 2 stands; "Appendix D.1 sums to 304/23 files" — it summed exactly 329/25). The refutations validate the cross-verify loop: expert auditors also confabulate.

**Decisions (all executed 2026-07-02):**
1. **Threat model must be disclosed wherever the safety axis is claimed.** HarmBench ran the `standard` config = direct harmful requests, NO attack/jailbreak augmentation (≈ DirectRequest, the weakest HarmBench threat model). Report v5 now states this in the abstract, Ch3 (boundary paragraph), §6.10, §7.1/§7.2 (external-validity First), Ch8 (first-class limitation), and Ch9 (attack arm = highest-leverage future work); deployment guidance hedged to BitsAndBytes + direct requests.
2. **The canonical report SOURCE is stale-scanned.** The audit's biggest catch — §6.13 presented retired 128-era κ as 512 results (judge-vs-proxy 0.19/0.11 and cross-judge 0.60–0.63; true 512 values 0.28/0.25 and 0.83/0.78, contradicting the report's own Table 6.3) — survived every gate because `scripts/*.js` was never in `stale_text.scan_paths`. `build_fyp_report_v5.js` is now scanned (retired builders/thesis builders excluded as history); retired-κ guards added (fire unless 128-scoped, self-tested); historical docx names in the builder's changelog are superseded-exempt.
3. **Point-in-time deliverables carry data-snapshot banners until mirrored.** All three tracked thesis docx asserted the retired +0.055 headline as current; every thesis builder now embeds a page-1 red DATA SNAPSHOT banner (headline superseded, see report v5) and the docx are rebuilt. The 512 thesis mirror remains open work.
4. **Evidence guards must be physical, not lexical.** `is_protected_results_dir` was bypassable via case-variant paths on the case-insensitive macOS filesystem (`RESULTS` == `results` by inode), which would have let the dashboard's force-restart smoke path delete canonical raw.jsonl. The guard now matches by device+inode AND case-folded names; the Run page resolves every execution dir through a single guarded choke point (`resolve_execution_dir`); regression-tested. Relatedly, the immutable gate now **fails** on partial local deletion of manifest files (was a non-blocking warn) — it detects destruction, not only mutation — and the redaction scan covers the committed sidecars/analysis trees.
5. **Smaller corrections, all verified in the rebuilt docx (18 content checks):** §6.16 discloses the 9.2% prefix-mismatch class (cross-run greedy divergence, llama-concentrated; within-run deltas unaffected; 60.3% is a floor) and the per-family truncation heterogeneity (llama 3–4% vs mistral 93.5–98%); §6.6.1/§6.16 disclose the qwen_2b multiseed sign-consistency (all 5 seed deltas ≥ 0, sub-MDE); reproducibility claim scoped (raws are local-only, hash-pinned; re-run-from-scratch or replay, not recompute-from-raw on a clone); provenance fields `quant_method`/`torch_dtype` persisted in future summary.json + boundary noted in the report; LOC corrected (~2,800/1,800 → ~8,900/4,600); test counts re-based to **338**; the v4-era "62%" (length-ceiling proxy) disambiguated from 60.3% (prefix test); float tolerance in `sensitivity_analysis.py` (llama greedy −0.040 now correctly in-range, JSON re-emitted); `docx` pinned in package.json (fresh-clone `make report` works); `tc1_int8_512.yaml` stale baseline comment fixed.

References [D41], [D42], [D16]. Follow-ups: claim-by-claim source-backed verification ledger (in progress); 512 thesis mirror; optional attack arm (GCG/PAIR subset) + GGUF pair for publication-grade external validity.

### D44. 2026-07-08 - Pre-submission audit: unify the significance criterion on McNemar's exact test (Qwen-1.7B ΔOR → borderline); persist per-seed evidence; fix the Llama-INT8 artefact mechanism

**Context:** a full pre-submission adversarial audit (8 independent examiner lenses — methodology, statistics, citations, results-interpretation, overclaiming, reproducibility/appendices, internal consistency, LLM-eval-standards — every finding adversarially verified against primary artifacts/code/papers; 27 raised → 11 confirmed + 1 plausible, **15 refuted**, plus 2 orchestrator-found defects no examiner raised). Nothing invalidates any result; all confirmed defects were consistency/appendix issues. All 12 fixed same-day.

**Decisions:**
1. **Significance criterion unified: McNemar's exact paired test decides significance for every paired-binary endpoint (HarmBench, XSTest, MMLU, ARC); the bootstrap CI is the interval-estimation layer.** Where the two disagree at the margin the delta is reported as *borderline*. Exactly one contrast sits there: **Qwen3-1.7B XSTest ΔOR = −0.028 (bootstrap CI [−0.052, −0.004] excludes zero, but McNemar p = 0.065 on 11 discordant prompts) — now "borderline", no longer "significant"**. This resolves the report-vs-thesis contradiction the audit found (report Table 6.1 said Sig=yes / "two significant over-refusal deltas"; thesis said only Phi is exact-test-significant) in favour of the exact test — consistent with the report's own §3.7 preference. RQ2 now reads: one significant over-refusal decrease (Phi, survives FDR) + one borderline decrease (Qwen 1.7B); headline unchanged (both point the benign way). User chose this over keeping the bootstrap verdict.
2. **Per-seed multiseed evidence must be persisted, not just stated.** §6.6.1's per-seed delta list and "k/5 seeds significant" counts were computed but stored nowhere. `scripts/sensitivity_analysis.py` now emits `judge_delta.per_seed` (per-seed delta, b, c, exact-McNemar p, significance) + `n_seeds_significant_p05` into the committed `results_512/analysis/sensitivity_multiseed.json` (re-emitted; aggregates byte-identical). Independent recomputation confirmed the report's claims exactly (qwen_2b 0/5, qwen_4b 1/5; llama has 2/5 individually significant seeds — both decreases, now disclosed in §6.6.1).
3. **The Llama-INT8 128-era signal is a cross-run-divergence artefact, not a truncation artefact.** §6.15 (and thesis §6/§8) had attributed its vanishing at 512 to "truncated generations", contradicting the study's own genlen data (Llama truncates 3–4%, the lowest family; it carries the highest prefix-mismatch share). Reworded to budget-sensitive cross-run greedy divergence; Qwen-1.7B's +0.055 remains correctly truncation-attributed.
4. **Appendix A now reproduces `configs/tc1_512.yaml`** (the primary-study config, correctly labelled, log_dir fixed) instead of a tc1.yaml/tc1_512 hybrid; a claim-lock check pins the appendix block to the on-disk file.
5. Other confirmed fixes: stale "text-only derivatives of a multimodal Qwen series" limitation replaced with a real one (**model revisions not commit-pinned** — also disclosed in §5.7); abstract no longer claims the power analysis "converges" on the capability reading (it bounds undetected effects); abstract "strictly contains" → "very nearly contains" (matches §6.12's judge_harmful_v2_not ≈ 0 phrasing); the multiseed T=0.7/top-p 0.8 setting attributed to Qwen3's card and disclosed as applied uniformly (Meta's Llama guidance is 0.6/0.9); Ch5 setup extended to the 5-pair/10-model reality (2026-06-15 second prefetch incl. gated Mistral, 4 extra matrix jobs, newpairs judge sbatch, 512 rerun); Appendix C schema summary gains `quant_method`; Appendix D check-count made self-describing ("55+; the gate prints its exact count").
6. **Gates extended:** claim lock 55 → **58 checks** (borderline verdict ↔ artifacts; per-seed list + counts ↔ artifact; Appendix A ↔ tc1_512.yaml) and 3 new stale-text patterns (retired "two significant over-refusal deltas" phrasing, the old Table-6.1 "yes" row, un-scoped "−0.028 … significant" in over-refusal context) — self-tested; the prose pattern caught one live residual (§6.3 "the only significant deltas are decreases") on its first run.

**Notable refutations (do not re-raise):** "judge-validated" is defensibly scoped (§6.12/§7.4 claim judge-vs-regex disagreement, not human ground truth — the no-human-gold-set limitation is already explicit); regex-scored XSTest is a sanctioned evaluation method in Röttger et al.; BH-FDR family composition is robust to re-derivation; the reported torch/transformers versions exist. References [D41], [D42], [D43], [D16].

### D42. 2026-07-02 - Claim-surface discipline: truth-changing edits require a repo-wide sweep of RESULT claims, machine-guarded

**Decision:** whenever a change alters what is *true* (headline numbers, significance verdicts, the primary configuration), the change is not complete until the repo-wide **claim surface** is swept — README, RESULTS_CARD, PROJECT_LOG §1, AGENTS/CLAUDE method text, `.github/assets` figure copies, HTML decks, dashboard data layer, todo, email drafts — by grepping for the old *numbers/claims* (not just old filenames), and the invariant is added to the machine gate (`artifact_policy.yaml` stale-text patterns, self-tested). Passing gates may only be cited for what they actually test. **Rationale:** during the D41 re-base, three external (Codex) audits successively found stale 128-era claims (+0.055 as current) in surfaces outside the report builder, after diff-scoped verification workflows had converged to "0 issues" — the verification perimeter was the diff, not the truth. Generalises D40. Rule recorded in AGENTS/CLAUDE ("When a RESULT changes, sweep the claim surface"); guards live (un-scoped `+0.055` lines; retired headline phrasing); a proactive full-repo sweep on 2026-07-02 then caught 6 further 128-era surfaces (decks, paper outline, dashboard tree default) that all three audits had missed.

### D41. 2026-06-30 - Promote 512-token to the PRIMARY study (HarmBench reference budget); 128 demoted to robustness comparison

> Note: originally logged as "D40" — renumbered to D41 on 2026-07-01 to resolve a duplicate-D40 collision with the 2026-06-29 v3-canonical decision above (found in the 2026-07-01 audit).

**Context:** D39 ran the full study at 512 tokens as a generation-length robustness check, keeping 128 primary. The 512 main analysis (phase E, verified) found the Qwen-1.7B headline ΔASR (+0.055 @128) does not replicate @512 (0.000 classifier / +0.005 gpt-4o, n.s., McNemar p=1.000, symmetric 16/16 flips); nothing survives BH-FDR @512 under either judge (κ 0.68–0.95); capability deltas budget-robust; 62% of 128-token responses were truncated.

**Decision (user, 2026-06-30):** promote **512 to the PRIMARY study** and demote 128 to the robustness comparison. Rationale: HarmBench's official classifier/evaluation pipeline uses a 512-token budget as its reference, so scoring the study's primary HarmBench ASR at 512 aligns it with the benchmark's own standard, and the 128-token run demonstrably truncated the majority (62%) of generations. I recommended the opposite (keep 128 primary + 512 as the §6.16 robustness layer: less rework, the 128-vs-512 contrast is itself the contribution, and 512 currently lacks the full apparatus); the user overrode, choosing 512-primary with a full-apparatus rerun.

**Scope / feasibility:** NOT a re-generation — generation + both judges at 512 are already done (D39). The "full apparatus at 512" is ~90% local analysis recomputes (per-category ASR breakdown, MMLU subject breakdown, judge agreement, multiple-comparisons/FDR, precision sweep, figures) pointed at `results_512/`, plus the already-prepared multi-seed jobs on TC1 (`slurm/jobs_tc1_sensitivity_512/`). The §6.14 refusal-margin mechanism probe is generation-length-invariant (first-token forward pass on the prompt; `max_new_tokens` does not affect it), so `results/analysis/refusal_margin.*` carries over unchanged. Re-scopes T31 from "robustness" to "primary"; the 128 `results/` tree is retained immutable. Execution plan in `todo.md` [2026-06-30]. References [D39], [D16].

### D39. 2026-06-29 - Full 512-token generation-length rerun, retaining the 128-token study (parallel results_512/ root)

**Context:** while building the T30 human-label tool, the user asked why HarmBench responses look "half-baked." Diagnosis: the study generates with `max_new_tokens=128` (documented, uniform across all configs + raw records; 0 rows clipped by sheet caps). HarmBench's own reference pipeline uses **512**, and HarmBench docs state generation length "drastically impacts ASR" (verified via web: centerforaisafety/HarmBench evaluation_pipeline.md + arXiv:2402.04249).

**Assessment given to the user:** 128 is a *conservative, defensible, disclosed* choice, not an error — the matched-pair ΔASR design absorbs a shared truncation budget, and the bias direction is conservative for the safety story (truncation hides late-arriving harmful content → cannot manufacture the finding). I recommended a **scoped** 512 sensitivity check on the headline pair (mirroring T18/T29). 

**Decision (user override, eyes-open):** do a **full** 512 rerun of the entire study (all 4 benchmarks; main fp16+NF4 + INT8 sweep + multi-seed), and **retain all 128-token data**. Rationale the user accepted: maximal confidence + the 128-vs-512 contrast itself becomes a robustness contribution. **Architecture:** a parallel `results_512/` root (proven by the existing `results_sensitivity/` pattern) — every 512 job passes `--output_dir results_512` + `configs/tc1_512.yaml` (`max_new_tokens: 512`); nothing in `results/` (the 128 originals + sha256 manifest) is ever touched. Tracked as **T31** with a 7-phase plan (A main matrix → B judge → C INT8 → D multi-seed → E re-analysis+comparison → F redo T30 on 512 → G report/thesis @512). Cost acknowledged: reopens every number, both judges, T30, and the report/thesis; multi-day TC1. References [D16] (judge-primary), [D35] (INT8), [T18] (sensitivity pattern), [T30] (paused pending this). The scoped-vs-full tradeoff was presented twice; the user chose full.
